Pot: ${itr?potAmt+'bb':'$'+potAmt}.`, label:'PLO Flop: facing bet with wrap draw'}; }}, {cat:'bluffing', name:'PLO river bluff or give up', build({itr,bb,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}){ const pos=randFrom(['BTN','CO']); const hand=drawPLOHand(['strong','playable']); const board=drawBoard(hand.cards,5); const potAmt=itr?bb*30:Math.round(bb*30); const correct='Give up and check (PLO river bluffs require near-nut blockers)'; return{cards:hand.cards,heroPos:pos,allPos,seats,board,street:'River', pfHist:`3-bet pot pre, c-bet flop, check turn. River: ${bStr([board[4]])}. Villain checks to hero.`, pot:itr?`${potAmt}bb`:`$${potAmt}`,callAmt:'0',blindStr,stackStr, correct,wrong:['Overbet bluff pot (polarized range)','Give up and check (PLO river bluffs require near-nut blockers)','Bet 50% pot bluff','Small block bet 33% pot'].filter(o=>o!==correct).slice(0,3), key:hand.handName, rangeNote:`${hand.handName} — PLO river bluff spot`, pfCtx:`PLO. Hero in ${pos} with ${hand.handName}. Board: ${bStr(board)}. Villain's calling range is very wide in PLO — bluffing rivers without near-nut blockers is -EV. Pot: ${itr?potAmt+'bb':'$'+potAmt}.`, label:'PLO River: bluff or give up'}; }} ]; // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // SCENARIO DISPATCHER // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function buildScenario(cat,game,itr){ const bb=itr?100:2; const stack=itr?randFrom([20,30,40,50,60,80,100])*bb:randFrom([100,150,200,300,500]); const stackStr=itr?stack+'bb':'$'+stack; const blindStr=itr?'50/100':'1/2'; const seats=randFrom([6,6,6,8,9]); const allPos=buildPos(seats); const ctx={itr,bb,stack,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}; if(game==='plo'){ const pool=cat==='preflop'?PLO_PF:[...PLO_POST.filter(t=>t.cat===cat||t.cat==='both'),...PLO_POST]; const tmpl=randFrom(pool.length?pool:PLO_POST); return{...tmpl.build(ctx),game:'PLO',variant:'PLO'}; } const pfPool=NLH_PF; const postPool=NLH_POST.filter(t=>cat==='bluffing'?t.cat==='bluffing':t.cat==='postflop'); const pool=cat==='preflop'?pfPool:(postPool.length?postPool:NLH_POST); const tmpl=randFrom(pool); return{...tmpl.build(ctx),game:'NLH',variant:"Texas Hold'em"}; } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // STATE & STORAGE // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ const state={variant:'holdem',format:'cash',cat:'preflop',difficulty:'Intermediate',villain:'TAG',showPotOdds:false,sessionMode:false,sessionCount:0,sessionAnswers:[],user:null,users:[],quiz:null,selected:null,loading:false,streak:0,hintUsed:false,hint:null}; const saveUsers=u=>S.set('upc:users',u); const loadProfile=id=>S.get('upc:p:'+id); const saveProfile=(id,d)=>S.set('upc:p:'+id,d); function emptyProfile(name){return{name,sessions:0,totalQ:0,totalCorrect:0,cats:{preflop:{q:0,c:0},postflop:{q:0,c:0},bluffing:{q:0,c:0}},history:[],streakBest:0,handLog:[]};} function getKey(){return localStorage.getItem('upc_api_key')||'';} async function callClaude(sys,msg,max){ const key=getKey(); const col=isRed?'#dc2626':'#1e293b'; const sym=SYM[suit]||suit; const fs=Math.round(w*0.35); const rs=Math.round(w*0.28); const rx=Math.round(w*0.12); return ` ${rank} ${sym} ${rank}`; } function tableHTML(quiz){ const cx=300,cy=155,rx=215,ry=105; Stack: ${stackStr}.`, label:`PLO Preflop: RFI from ${pos}`}; }}, {name:'PLO 3-bet or call', build({itr,bb,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}){ const op=randFrom(['UTG','MP','HJ','CO','BTN']); const hero=randFrom(['CO','BTN','SB','BB'].filter(p=>p!==op)); const isPrem=Math.random()>0.45; const hand=drawPLOHand(isPrem?['premium']:['strong','playable']); const correct=isPrem?`3-bet pot to ${itr?Math.round(11*bb)+'bb':'$'+Math.round(11*bb)}`:'Call (flat and see flop in position)'; return{cards:hand.cards,heroPos:hero,allPos,seats,board:[],street:'Preflop', pfHist:`${op} pot-raises to ${itr?'3.5bb':'$'+Math.round(3.5*bb)}. Folds to hero in ${hero}.`, pot:itr?`${bb*8}bb`:`$${Math.round(bb*8)}`,callAmt:itr?`${Math.round(3.5*bb)}bb`:`$${Math.round(3.5*bb)}`,blindStr,stackStr, correct,wrong:['Call (flat and see flop in position)',`3-bet pot to ${itr?Math.round(11*bb)+'bb':'$'+Math.round(11*bb)}`,'Fold',`Min-raise to ${itr?'5bb':'$'+Math.round(5*bb)}`].filter(o=>o!==correct).slice(0,3), key:hand.handName, rangeNote:`${hand.handName} — PLO ${isPrem?'✓ 3-bet premium':'✓ Call strong hand'}`, pfCtx:`PLO. ${op} opens pot. Hero in ${hero} with ${hand.handName} (${hand.desc}). Stack: ${stackStr}.`, label:`PLO Preflop: ${hero} facing ${op} open`}; }} ]; const PLO_POST = [ {cat:'postflop', name:'PLO top set vs draw board', build({itr,bb,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}){ const pos=randFrom(['BTN','CO']); const hand=drawPLOHand(['premium']); const board=drawBoard(hand.cards,3); const tex=boardTex(board); const correct=tex==='wet'?'Bet pot (charge draws — critical in PLO)':'Bet 66% pot (value, semi-dry board)'; return{cards:hand.cards,heroPos:pos,allPos,seats,board,street:'Flop', pfHist:`3-bet pot pre. Hero in ${pos}. Flop: ${bStr(board)}. Villain checks.`, pot:itr?`${bb*8}bb`:`$${Math.round(bb*8)}`,callAmt:'0',blindStr,stackStr, correct,wrong:['Check (pot control)','Bet 33% pot','Bet pot (charge draws — critical in PLO)','Bet 66% pot (value, semi-dry board)'].filter(o=>o!==correct).slice(0,3), key:hand.handName,tex, rangeNote:`${hand.handName} — PLO flop (${tex})`, pfCtx:`PLO 3-bet pot. Hero in ${pos} with ${hand.handName}. Flop: ${bStr(board)} (${tex}). In PLO draws have massive equity — charge immediately. Pot: ${itr?bb*8+'bb':'$'+Math.round(bb*8)}.`, label:`PLO Flop: set on ${tex} board`}; }}, {cat:'postflop', name:'PLO wrap draw decision', build({itr,bb,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}){ const hand=drawPLOHand(['strong','playable']); const board=drawBoard(hand.cards,3); const tex=boardTex(board); const potAmt=itr?bb*7:Math.round(bb*7); const betA=itr?`${Math.round(potAmt)}bb`:`$${potAmt}`; const correct='Call (wraps have ~60% equity vs sets — need implied odds)'; return{cards:hand.cards,heroPos:'BB',allPos,seats,board,street:'Flop', pfHist:`Opponent pot-bets ${betA} on ${bStr(board)}. Hero in BB with wrap draw potential.`, pot:itr?`${potAmt}bb`:`$${potAmt}`,callAmt:betA,blindStr,stackStr, correct,wrong:['Fold (draws are weak in PLO)','Raise pot (semi-bluff re-raise)','Call (wraps have ~60% equity vs sets — need implied odds)','Fold unless also have nut flush draw'].filter(o=>o!==correct).slice(0,3), key:hand.handName,tex, rangeNote:`${hand.handName} — PLO wrap draw on ${bStr(board)}`, pfCtx:`PLO. Hero in BB with ${hand.handName} (${hand.desc}). Facing pot-bet on ${bStr(board)}. PLO wraps can have 13-20 outs and ~60% equity vs top set. Pot: ${itr?potAmt+'bb':'$'+potAmt}.`, label:'PLO Flop: facing bet with wrap draw'}; }}, {cat:'bluffing', name:'PLO river bluff or give up', build({itr,bb,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}){ const pos=randFrom(['BTN','CO']); const hand=drawPLOHand(['strong','playable']); const board=drawBoard(hand.cards,5); const potAmt=itr?bb*30:Math.round(bb*30); const correct='Give up and check (PLO river bluffs require near-nut blockers)'; return{cards:hand.cards,heroPos:pos,allPos,seats,board,street:'River', pfHist:`3-bet pot pre, c-bet flop, check turn. River: ${bStr([board[4]])}. Villain checks to hero.`, pot:itr?`${potAmt}bb`:`$${potAmt}`,callAmt:'0',blindStr,stackStr, correct,wrong:['Overbet bluff pot (polarized range)','Give up and check (PLO river bluffs require near-nut blockers)','Bet 50% pot bluff','Small block bet 33% pot'].filter(o=>o!==correct).slice(0,3), key:hand.handName, rangeNote:`${hand.handName} — PLO river bluff spot`, pfCtx:`PLO. Hero in ${pos} with ${hand.handName}. Board: ${bStr(board)}. Villain's calling range is very wide in PLO — bluffing rivers without near-nut blockers is -EV. Pot: ${itr?potAmt+'bb':'$'+potAmt}.`, label:'PLO River: bluff or give up'}; }} ]; // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // SCENARIO DISPATCHER // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function buildScenario(cat,game,itr){ const bb=itr?100:2; const stack=itr?randFrom([20,30,40,50,60,80,100])*bb:randFrom([100,150,200,300,500]); const stackStr=itr?stack+'bb':'$'+stack; const blindStr=itr?'50/100':'1/2'; const seats=randFrom([6,6,6,8,9]); const allPos=buildPos(seats); const ctx={itr,bb,stack,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}; if(game==='plo'){ const pool=cat==='preflop'?PLO_PF:[...PLO_POST.filter(t=>t.cat===cat||t.cat==='both'),...PLO_POST]; const tmpl=randFrom(pool.length?pool:PLO_POST); return{...tmpl.build(ctx),game:'PLO',variant:'PLO'}; } const pfPool=NLH_PF; const postPool=NLH_POST.filter(t=>cat==='bluffing'?t.cat==='bluffing':t.cat==='postflop'); const pool=cat==='preflop'?pfPool:(postPool.length?postPool:NLH_POST); const tmpl=randFrom(pool); return{...tmpl.build(ctx),game:'NLH',variant:"Texas Hold'em"}; } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // STATE & STORAGE // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ const state={variant:'holdem',format:'cash',cat:'preflop',difficulty:'Intermediate',villain:'TAG',showPotOdds:false,sessionMode:false,sessionCount:0,sessionAnswers:[],user:null,users:[],quiz:null,selected:null,loading:false,streak:0,hintUsed:false,hint:null}; const S={get:k=>{try{const v=localStorage.getItem(k);return v?JSON.parse(v):null;}catch{return null;}},set:(k,v)=>{try{localStorage.setItem(k,JSON.stringify(v));}catch{}}}; const loadUsers=()=>S.get('upc:users')||[]; const saveUsers=u=>S.set('upc:users',u); const loadProfile=id=>S.get('upc:p:'+id); const saveProfile=(id,d)=>S.set('upc:p:'+id,d); function emptyProfile(name){return{name,sessions:0,totalQ:0,totalCorrect:0,cats:{preflop:{q:0,c:0},postflop:{q:0,c:0},bluffing:{q:0,c:0}},history:[],streakBest:0,handLog:[]};} function getKey(){return localStorage.getItem('upc_api_key')||'';} async function callClaude(sys,msg,max){ const key=getKey(); if(!key)throw new Error('No API key.'); const r=await fetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages',{method:'POST',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json','x-api-key':key,'anthropic-version':'2023-06-01','anthropic-dangerous-direct-browser-access':'true'},body:JSON.stringify({model:'claude-sonnet-4-20250514',max_tokens:max||900,system:sys,messages:[{role:'user',content:msg}]})}); const d=await r.json(); if(d.error)throw new Error(d.error.message); return d.content.map(i=>i.text||'').join(''); } function startApp(){ const key=(document.getElementById('api-key').value||'').trim(); const err=document.getElementById('gate-err'); err.style.display='none'; if(!key){err.textContent='Please enter your API key.';err.style.display='block';return;} if(!key.startsWith('sk-ant-')){err.textContent='Invalid key — should start with sk-ant-';err.style.display='block';return;} localStorage.setItem('upc_api_key',key); if(saved&&saved.startsWith('sk-ant-')){launchApp();} const inp=document.getElementById('api-key'); if(inp)inp.addEventListener('keydown',e=>{if(e.key==='Enter')startApp();}); }); function showUserSelect(){ let html=`

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // FETCH QUIZ // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ async function fetchQuiz(){ if(!state.user)return; state.loading=true;state.quiz=null;state.selected=null;state.hintUsed=false;state.hint=null; renderQuiz(); try{ const itr=state.format==='tournament'; const game=state.variant==='mixed'?(Math.random()>0.5?'plo':'nlh'):state.variant==='plo'?'plo':'nlh'; const ctx=buildScenario(state.cat,game,itr); const allOpts=shuffle([ctx.correct,...ctx.wrong].slice(0,4)); const correctIdx=allOpts.indexOf(ctx.correct); const diffDesc={Beginner:'Simple explanation, basic concepts.',Intermediate:'Reference position, ranges, pot odds.',Advanced:'GTO-level: MDF, polarization, blockers, solver frequencies.'}[state.difficulty]||''; const isPLO=game==='plo'; const sys=`You are an expert ${isPLO?'PLO':'NL Hold\'em'} GTO poker coach. The hand setup, preflop action history, and correct answer are already determined by a range engine — do NOT change them. Write a 2-sentence scenario description and 3-4 sentence GTO explanation based exactly on what is given. Villain type: ${state.villain}. ${diffDesc}${isPLO?' Reference PLO-specific concepts: wraps, nut flush draws, multi-way equity.':''} Respond ONLY valid JSON, no markdown: {"scenario":"2 sentences","explanation":"3-4 sentences GTO reasoning","hintText":"1 sentence hint without revealing answer"}`; const prompt=`Game: ${ctx.variant}. Format: ${itr?'Tournament':'Cash'}. Hero: ${ctx.heroPos}. Hole cards: ${ctx.cards.map(c=>c.rank+c.suit).join(' ')} (${ctx.key}). Action (use exactly this): ${ctx.pfCtx} Preflop history: ${ctx.pfHist} Board: ${ctx.board?.length?bStr(ctx.board):'(preflop — no board)'} Correct answer: ${ctx.correct} Wrong options: ${ctx.wrong.join(' / ')} Range note: ${ctx.rangeNote}`; const txt=await callClaude(sys,prompt,800); const parsed=JSON.parse(txt.replace(/```json|```/g,'').trim()); const potAmt=parseDollar(ctx.pot||'0'); const callAmt=parseDollar(ctx.callAmt||'0'); const ratio=callAmt>0?((potAmt+callAmt)/callAmt).toFixed(1)+':1':'N/A'; const bePct=callAmt>0?Math.round((callAmt/(potAmt+callAmt))*100)+'%':'N/A'; state.quiz={ variant:ctx.variant,gameType:itr?'Tournament':'Cash Game', street:ctx.street,heroPosition:ctx.heroPos, numSeats:ctx.seats,allPositions:ctx.allPos, stackSizes:buildStacks(ctx.seats,itr),bets:{}, potDisplay:ctx.pot,blinds:ctx.blindStr, holeCards:ctx.cards, // ← always ctx.cards (never undefined) communityCards:ctx.board||[], scenario:parsed.scenario,question:'What is the correct GTO action?', options:allOpts,correctIndex:correctIdx, explanation:parsed.explanation,hintText:parsed.hintText, rangeNote:ctx.rangeNote,actionLabel:ctx.label, potOdds:callAmt>0?{potSize:ctx.pot,callAmount:'$'+callAmt,oddsRatio:ratio,breakEvenPct:bePct,impliedOdds:isPLO?'PLO implied odds massive with wraps+flush draws':'Consider stack depth and villain tendencies',recommendation:callAmt/(potAmt+callAmt)<0.33?'Fold (insufficient pot odds)':'Call (pot odds sufficient)'}:null }; }catch(e){state.quiz={error:true,msg:e.message||'Unknown error'};} state.loading=false; renderQuiz(); } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // CARD & TABLE RENDERING // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function cardSVG(rank, suit, x, y, w, h){ // Renders a single card as SVG elements at position x,y with size w x h const isRed=suit==='h'||suit==='d'; const col=isRed?'#dc2626':'#1e293b'; const sym=SYM[suit]||suit; const fs=Math.round(w*0.35); const rs=Math.round(w*0.28); const rx=Math.round(w*0.12); return ` ${rank} ${sym} ${rank}`; } function tableHTML(quiz){ const cx=300,cy=155,rx=215,ry=105; const seats=quiz.numSeats||6; const posLabels=quiz.allPositions||buildPos(seats); const heroPos=quiz.heroPosition||''; const stacks=quiz.stackSizes||[]; const holeCards=quiz.holeCards||[]; // guaranteed array const cc=quiz.communityCards||[]; let inner=` `; // Community cards if(cc.length>0){ const cw=36,ch=50,gap=5; const totalW=cc.length*cw+(cc.length-1)*gap; const sx=cx-totalW/2, sy=cy-ch/2; cc.forEach((c,i)=>{inner+=cardSVG(c.rank,c.suit,sx+i*(cw+gap),sy,cw,ch);}); if(quiz.potDisplay&&quiz.potDisplay!=='$0') inner+=`POT ${quiz.potDisplay}`; } else if(quiz.potDisplay&&quiz.potDisplay!=='$0'){ inner+=` POT ${quiz.potDisplay}`; } // Seats for(let i=0;i`; // Dealer button if(isBtn) inner+=`D`; // Position label inner+=`${label}`; // YOU label if(isHero) inner+=`YOU`; // Stack size if(stack) inner+=`${stack}`; // Hero hole cards — rendered below the seat if(isHero && holeCards.length>0){ const isPLO=holeCards.length===4; const cw=isPLO?20:26, ch=isPLO?29:37, cgap=3; const totalCW=holeCards.length*cw+(holeCards.length-1)*cgap; const hcX=sx-totalCW/2; const hcY=sy+(stack?52:46); holeCards.forEach((c,ci)=>{ inner+=cardSVG(c.rank,c.suit,hcX+ci*(cw+cgap),hcY,cw,ch); }); } } return `
`; } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // RENDER QUIZ // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function renderQuiz(){ const area=document.getElementById('quiz-area');if(!area)return; if(state.loading){area.innerHTML=`

`; if(state.selected!==null){ const ok=state.selected===q.correctIndex; html+=`

Pot: ${itr?potAmt+'bb':'$'+potAmt}.`, label:'Turn: barrel or check IP'}; }}, {cat:'postflop', name:'River value bet or check', build({itr,bb,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}){ const pos=randFrom(['BTN','CO']); const cards=drawFrom(NLRFI[pos]||NLRFI.BTN); const board=drawBoard(cards,5); const str=nlStr(cards[0],cards[1],board.slice(0,3)); const correct=str==='monster'?'Bet 100% pot (max value)':str==='strong'?'Bet 66% pot (3-street value)':str==='medium'?'Check back (marginal SDV)':'Check back (missed draw, no value)'; const potAmt=itr?bb*36:Math.round(bb*36); return{cards,heroPos:pos,allPos,seats,board,street:'River', pfHist:`3-bet pot. Stack: ${stackStr}.`, label:`PLO Preflop: ${hero} facing ${op} open`}; }} ]; const PLO_POST = [ {cat:'postflop', name:'PLO top set vs draw board', build({itr,bb,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}){ const pos=randFrom(['BTN','CO']); const hand=drawPLOHand(['premium']); const board=drawBoard(hand.cards,3); const tex=boardTex(board); const correct=tex==='wet'?'Bet pot (charge draws — critical in PLO)':'Bet 66% pot (value, semi-dry board)'; return{cards:hand.cards,heroPos:pos,allPos,seats,board,street:'Flop', pfHist:`3-bet pot pre. const stack=itr?randFrom([20,30,40,50,60,80,100])*bb:randFrom([100,150,200,300,500]); const stackStr=itr?stack+'bb':'$'+stack; const blindStr=itr?'50/100':'1/2'; const seats=randFrom([6,6,6,8,9]); const allPos=buildPos(seats); const ctx={itr,bb,stack,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}; if(game==='plo'){ const pool=cat==='preflop'?PLO_PF:[...PLO_POST.filter(t=>t.cat===cat||t.cat==='both'),...PLO_POST]; const tmpl=randFrom(pool.length?pool:PLO_POST); return{...tmpl.build(ctx),game:'PLO',variant:'PLO'}; } const pfPool=NLH_PF; const postPool=NLH_POST.filter(t=>cat==='bluffing'?t.cat==='bluffing':t.cat==='postflop'); const pool=cat==='preflop'?pfPool:(postPool.length?postPool:NLH_POST); const tmpl=randFrom(pool); return{...tmpl.build(ctx),game:'NLH',variant:"Texas Hold'em"}; } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // STATE & STORAGE // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ const state={variant:'holdem',format:'cash',cat:'preflop',difficulty:'Intermediate',villain:'TAG',showPotOdds:false,sessionMode:false,sessionCount:0,sessionAnswers:[],user:null,users:[],quiz:null,selected:null,loading:false,streak:0,hintUsed:false,hint:null}; const S={get:k=>{try{const v=localStorage.getItem(k);return v?JSON.parse(v):null;}catch{return null;}},set:(k,v)=>{try{localStorage.setItem(k,JSON.stringify(v));}catch{}}}; const loadUsers=()=>S.get('upc:users')||[]; const saveUsers=u=>S.set('upc:users',u); const loadProfile=id=>S.get('upc:p:'+id); const saveProfile=(id,d)=>S.set('upc:p:'+id,d); function emptyProfile(name){return{name,sessions:0,totalQ:0,totalCorrect:0,cats:{preflop:{q:0,c:0},postflop:{q:0,c:0},bluffing:{q:0,c:0}},history:[],streakBest:0,handLog:[]};} function getKey(){return localStorage.getItem('upc_api_key')||'';} async function callClaude(sys,msg,max){ const key=getKey(); if(!key)throw new Error('No API key.'); const r=await fetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages',{method:'POST',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json','x-api-key':key,'anthropic-version':'2023-06-01','anthropic-dangerous-direct-browser-access':'true'},body:JSON.stringify({model:'claude-sonnet-4-20250514',max_tokens:max||900,system:sys,messages:[{role:'user',content:msg}]})}); const d=await r.json(); if(d.error)throw new Error(d.error.message); return d.content.map(i=>i.text||'').join(''); } function startApp(){ const key=(document.getElementById('api-key').value||'').trim(); `; state.users.forEach(u=>{ const pct=u.totalQ?Math.round((u.totalCorrect/u.totalQ)*100):0; html+=``; }); html+=``; document.getElementById('overlay-content').innerHTML=html; document.getElementById('overlay').style.display='flex'; } function showAddUser(){ document.getElementById('overlay-content').innerHTML=`

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // FETCH QUIZ // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ async function fetchQuiz(){ if(!state.user)return; state.loading=true;state.quiz=null;state.selected=null;state.hintUsed=false;state.hint=null; renderQuiz(); try{ const itr=state.format==='tournament'; const game=state.variant==='mixed'?(Math.random()>0.5?'plo':'nlh'):state.variant==='plo'?'plo':'nlh'; const ctx=buildScenario(state.cat,game,itr); const allOpts=shuffle([ctx.correct,...ctx.wrong].slice(0,4)); const correctIdx=allOpts.indexOf(ctx.correct); const diffDesc={Beginner:'Simple explanation, basic concepts.',Intermediate:'Reference position, ranges, pot odds.',Advanced:'GTO-level: MDF, polarization, blockers, solver frequencies.'}[state.difficulty]||''; const isPLO=game==='plo'; const sys=`You are an expert ${isPLO?'PLO':'NL Hold\'em'} GTO poker coach. The hand setup, preflop action history, and correct answer are already determined by a range engine — do NOT change them. Write a 2-sentence scenario description and 3-4 sentence GTO explanation based exactly on what is given. Villain type: ${state.villain}. ${diffDesc}${isPLO?' Reference PLO-specific concepts: wraps, nut flush draws, multi-way equity.':''} Respond ONLY valid JSON, no markdown: {"scenario":"2 sentences","explanation":"3-4 sentences GTO reasoning","hintText":"1 sentence hint without revealing answer"}`; const prompt=`Game: ${ctx.variant}. Format: ${itr?'Tournament':'Cash'}. Hero: ${ctx.heroPos}. Hole cards: ${ctx.cards.map(c=>c.rank+c.suit).join(' ')} (${ctx.key}). Action (use exactly this): ${ctx.pfCtx} Preflop history: ${ctx.pfHist} Board: ${ctx.board?.length?bStr(ctx.board):'(preflop — no board)'} Correct answer: ${ctx.correct} Wrong options: ${ctx.wrong.join(' / ')} Range note: ${ctx.rangeNote}`; const txt=await callClaude(sys,prompt,800); const parsed=JSON.parse(txt.replace(/```json|```/g,'').trim()); const potAmt=parseDollar(ctx.pot||'0'); const callAmt=parseDollar(ctx.callAmt||'0'); const ratio=callAmt>0?((potAmt+callAmt)/callAmt).toFixed(1)+':1':'N/A'; const bePct=callAmt>0?Math.round((callAmt/(potAmt+callAmt))*100)+'%':'N/A'; state.quiz={ variant:ctx.variant,gameType:itr?'Tournament':'Cash Game', street:ctx.street,heroPosition:ctx.heroPos, numSeats:ctx.seats,allPositions:ctx.allPos, stackSizes:buildStacks(ctx.seats,itr),bets:{}, potDisplay:ctx.pot,blinds:ctx.blindStr, holeCards:ctx.cards, // ← always ctx.cards (never undefined) communityCards:ctx.board||[], scenario:parsed.scenario,question:'What is the correct GTO action?', options:allOpts,correctIndex:correctIdx, explanation:parsed.explanation,hintText:parsed.hintText, rangeNote:ctx.rangeNote,actionLabel:ctx.label, potOdds:callAmt>0?{potSize:ctx.pot,callAmount:'$'+callAmt,oddsRatio:ratio,breakEvenPct:bePct,impliedOdds:isPLO?'PLO implied odds massive with wraps+flush draws':'Consider stack depth and villain tendencies',recommendation:callAmt/(potAmt+callAmt)<0.33?'Fold (insufficient pot odds)':'Call (pot odds sufficient)'}:null }; }catch(e){state.quiz={error:true,msg:e.message||'Unknown error'};} state.loading=false; renderQuiz(); } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // CARD & TABLE RENDERING // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function cardSVG(rank, suit, x, y, w, h){ // Renders a single card as SVG elements at position x,y with size w x h const isRed=suit==='h'||suit==='d'; const col=isRed?'#dc2626':'#1e293b'; const sym=SYM[suit]||suit; const fs=Math.round(w*0.35); const rs=Math.round(w*0.28); const rx=Math.round(w*0.12); return ` ${rank} ${sym} ${rank}`; } function tableHTML(quiz){ const cx=300,cy=155,rx=215,ry=105; const seats=quiz.numSeats||6; const posLabels=quiz.allPositions||buildPos(seats); const heroPos=quiz.heroPosition||''; const stacks=quiz.stackSizes||[]; const holeCards=quiz.holeCards||[]; // guaranteed array const cc=quiz.communityCards||[]; let inner=` `; // Community cards if(cc.length>0){ const cw=36,ch=50,gap=5; const totalW=cc.length*cw+(cc.length-1)*gap; const sx=cx-totalW/2, sy=cy-ch/2; cc.forEach((c,i)=>{inner+=cardSVG(c.rank,c.suit,sx+i*(cw+gap),sy,cw,ch);}); if(quiz.potDisplay&&quiz.potDisplay!=='$0') inner+=`POT ${quiz.potDisplay}`; } else if(quiz.potDisplay&&quiz.potDisplay!=='$0'){ inner+=` POT ${quiz.potDisplay}`; } // Seats for(let i=0;i`; // Dealer button if(isBtn) inner+=`D`; // Position label inner+=`${label}`; // YOU label if(isHero) inner+=`YOU`; // Stack size if(stack) inner+=`${stack}`; // Hero hole cards — rendered below the seat if(isHero && holeCards.length>0){ const isPLO=holeCards.length===4; // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // FETCH QUIZ // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ async function fetchQuiz(){ if(!state.user)return; game=state.variant==='mixed'?(Math.random()>0.5?'plo':'nlh'):state.variant==='plo'?'plo':'nlh'; const ctx=buildScenario(state.cat,game,itr); const allOpts=shuffle([ctx.correct,...ctx.wrong].slice(0,4)); const correctIdx=allOpts.indexOf(ctx.correct); const diffDesc={Beginner:'Simple explanation, basic concepts.',Intermediate:'Reference position, ranges, pot odds.',Advanced:'GTO-level: MDF, polarization, blockers, solver frequencies.'}[state.difficulty]||''; const isPLO=game==='plo'; const sys=`You are an expert ${isPLO?'PLO':'NL Hold\'em'} SB vs single open (3-bet or fold, tight call range) {name:'SB vs single open', build({itr,bb,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}){ const op=randFrom(['HJ','CO','BTN']); const thr=NL3BET.vsBTN; const roll=Math.random(); let cards,correct; if(roll<0.40){cards=drawFrom(thr);correct=`3-bet to ${itr?'9bb':'$'+Math.round(bb*9)}`;} else if(roll<0.60){cards=drawFrom(NLSBCALL);const k=hkey(cards[0],cards[1]);correct=thr.has(k)?`3-bet to ${itr?'9bb':'$'+Math.round(bb*9)}`:`Call (tight SB flat — strong implied odds hand)`;} else{const fp=shuffle([...NLRFI.BTN].filter(k=>!thr.has(k)&&!NLSBCALL.has(k)));cards=decodeKey(fp[0]||'K7o');correct='Fold (SB is OOP — 3-bet or fold most hands)';} const key=hkey(cards[0],cards[1]); return{cards,heroPos:'SB',allPos,seats,board:[],street:'Preflop', pfHist:`${op} opens to ${itr?'2.5bb':'$'+Math.round(bb*2.5)}. Folds to hero in SB.`, pot:itr?`${bb*4}bb`:`$${Math.round(bb*4)}`,callAmt:itr?`${bb*1.5}bb`:`$${Math.round(bb*1.5)}`, blindStr,stackStr,correct,wrong:pfWrong(correct,itr,bb),key, rangeNote:`${key} — SB vs ${op}: ${correct.includes('Fold')?'✗ Fold OOP':correct.includes('3-bet')?'✓ 3-bet':'✓ Tight flat'}`, pfCtx:`${op} opens. Hero in SB with ${key}. SB is OOP and BB can squeeze — calling range is very tight. GTO: 3-bet strong hands, call only premium suited hands, fold the rest. Stack: ${stackStr}.`, label:`Preflop: SB facing ${op} open`}; }}, // 6. SB vs BB only — limp, raise, or fold (GTO limp spot #1) {name:'SB action vs BB only', build({itr,bb,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}){ const roll=Math.random(); let cards,correct; if(roll<0.38){cards=drawFrom(NLRFI.SB);correct=`Raise to ${itr?'3bb':'$'+Math.round(bb*3)}`;} else if(roll<0.72){cards=drawFrom(NLSBLMP);correct='Complete (limp) — GTO mixed strategy vs BB only';} else{const trash=['72o','73o','83o','82o','92o','J2o','Q2o','T2o'];cards=decodeKey(randFrom(trash));correct='Fold';} const key=hkey(cards[0],cards[1]); return{cards,heroPos:'SB',allPos,seats,board:[],street:'Preflop', pfHist:'Folds to hero in SB. BB facing SB limp — check or iso-raise (GTO limp spot #2) {name:'BB facing SB limp', build({itr,bb,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}){ const roll=Math.random(); let cards,correct; if(roll<0.40){cards=drawFrom(NLBBISO);correct=`Iso-raise to ${itr?'4bb':'$'+Math.round(bb*4)}`;} else{cards=drawFrom(NLBBDEF);const k=hkey(cards[0],cards[1]);correct=NLBBISO.has(k)&&Math.random()>0.55?`Iso-raise to ${itr?'4bb':'$'+Math.round(bb*4)}`:'Check (take free flop — never fold to a limp)';} const key=hkey(cards[0],cards[1]); return{cards,heroPos:'BB',allPos,seats,board:[],street:'Preflop', pfHist:'Folds to SB, SB completes (limps). const stack=itr?randFrom([20,30,40,50,60,80,100])*bb:randFrom([100,150,200,300,500]); const stackStr=itr?stack+'bb':'$'+stack; const blindStr=itr?'50/100':'1/2'; const seats=randFrom([6,6,6,8,9]); const allPos=buildPos(seats); const ctx={itr,bb,stack,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}; if(game==='plo'){ const pool=cat==='preflop'?PLO_PF:[...PLO_POST.filter(t=>t.cat===cat||t.cat==='both'),...PLO_POST]; const tmpl=randFrom(pool.length?pool:PLO_POST); return{...tmpl.build(ctx),game:'PLO',variant:'PLO'}; } const pfPool=NLH_PF; const postPool=NLH_POST.filter(t=>cat==='bluffing'?t.cat==='bluffing':t.cat==='postflop'); const pool=cat==='preflop'?pfPool:(postPool.length?postPool:NLH_POST); const tmpl=randFrom(pool); return{...tmpl.build(ctx),game:'NLH',variant:"Texas Hold'em"}; } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // STATE & STORAGE // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ const state={variant:'holdem',format:'cash',cat:'preflop',difficulty:'Intermediate',villain:'TAG',showPotOdds:false,sessionMode:false,sessionCount:0,sessionAnswers:[],user:null,users:[],quiz:null,selected:null,loading:false,streak:0,hintUsed:false,hint:null}; const S={get:k=>{try{const v=localStorage.getItem(k);return v?JSON.parse(v):null;}catch{return null;}},set:(k,v)=>{try{localStorage.setItem(k,JSON.stringify(v));}catch{}}}; const loadUsers=()=>S.get('upc:users')||[]; const saveUsers=u=>S.set('upc:users',u); const loadProfile=id=>S.get('upc:p:'+id); const saveProfile=(id,d)=>S.set('upc:p:'+id,d); function emptyProfile(name){return{name,sessions:0,totalQ:0,totalCorrect:0,cats:{preflop:{q:0,c:0},postflop:{q:0,c:0},bluffing:{q:0,c:0}},history:[],streakBest:0,handLog:[]};} function getKey(){return localStorage.getItem('upc_api_key')||'';} async function callClaude(sys,msg,max){ const key=getKey(); if(!key)throw new Error('No API key.'); const r=await fetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages',{method:'POST',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json','x-api-key':key,'anthropic-version':'2023-06-01','anthropic-dangerous-direct-browser-access':'true'},body:JSON.stringify({model:'claude-sonnet-4-20250514',max_tokens:max||900,system:sys,messages:[{role:'user',content:msg}]})}); const d=await r.json(); if(d.error)throw new Error(d.error.message); return d.content.map(i=>i.text||'').join(''); } function startApp(){ const key=(document.getElementById('api-key').value||'').trim(); const err=document.getElementById('gate-err'); err.style.display='none'; if(!key){err.textContent='Please enter your API key.';err.style.display='block';return;} if(!key.startsWith('sk-ant-')){err.textContent='Invalid key — should start with sk-ant-';err.style.display='block';return;} localStorage.setItem('upc_api_key',key); launchApp(); } function launchApp(){ document.getElementById('gate').style.display='none'; document.getElementById('app').style.display='flex'; state.users=loadUsers(); showUserSelect(); } window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',()=>{ const saved=localStorage.getItem('upc_api_key'); if(saved&&saved.startsWith('sk-ant-')){launchApp();} const inp=document.getElementById('api-key'); if(inp)inp.addEventListener('keydown',e=>{if(e.key==='Enter')startApp();}); }); function showUserSelect(){ let html=`
Upgrade Poker Coach
Select your profile
`; state.users.forEach(u=>{ const pct=u.totalQ?Math.round((u.totalCorrect/u.totalQ)*100):0; html+=``; }); html+=``; document.getElementById('overlay-content').innerHTML=html; document.getElementById('overlay').style.display='flex'; } function showAddUser(){ document.getElementById('overlay-content').innerHTML=`
Add Player
`; setTimeout(()=>{const n=document.getElementById('new-name');if(n)n.focus();},100); } function addUser(){ const name=(document.getElementById('new-name').value||'').trim(); const err=document.getElementById('name-err'); if(!name){err.textContent='Enter a name';err.style.display='block';return;} if(state.users.find(u=>u.name.toLowerCase()===name.toLowerCase())){err.textContent='Name taken';err.style.display='block';return;} const id='u_'+Date.now(); // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // FETCH QUIZ // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ async function fetchQuiz(){ if(!state.user)return; const bePct=callAmt>0?Math.round((callAmt/(potAmt+callAmt))*100)+'%':'N/A'; state.quiz={ variant:ctx.variant,gameType:itr?'Tournament':'Cash Game', street:ctx.street,heroPosition:ctx.heroPos, numSeats:ctx.seats,allPositions:ctx.allPos, stackSizes:buildStacks(ctx.seats,itr),bets:{}, potDisplay:ctx.pot,blinds:ctx.blindStr, holeCards:ctx.cards, // ← always ctx.cards (never undefined) communityCards:ctx.board||[], scenario:parsed.scenario,question:'What is the correct GTO action?', options:allOpts,correctIndex:correctIdx, explanation:parsed.explanation,hintText:parsed.hintText, rangeNote:ctx.rangeNote,actionLabel:ctx.label, potOdds:callAmt>0?{potSize:ctx.pot,callAmount:'$'+callAmt,oddsRatio:ratio,breakEvenPct:bePct,impliedOdds:isPLO?'PLO implied odds massive with wraps+flush draws':'Consider stack depth and villain tendencies',recommendation:callAmt/(potAmt+callAmt)<0.33?'Fold (insufficient pot odds)':'Call (pot odds sufficient)'}:null }; const col=isRed?'#dc2626':'#1e293b'; const sym=SYM[suit]||suit; const fs=Math.round(w*0.35); const rs=Math.round(w*0.28); const rx=Math.round(w*0.12); return ` ${rank} ${sym} ${rank}`; } function tableHTML(quiz){ const cx=300,cy=155,rx=215,ry=105; RFI — raise or fold {name:'RFI decision', build({itr,bb,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}){ const pos=randFrom(['UTG','MP','HJ','CO','BTN','SB']); const range=NLRFI[pos]||NLRFI.HJ; const inR=Math.random()>0.3; const cards=inR?drawFrom(range):drawFrom(new Set([...NLRFI.BTN].filter(k=>!range.has(k)))); const key=hkey(cards[0],cards[1]); const correct=inR?`Raise to ${itr?'2.5bb':'$'+Math.round(bb*2.5)}`:'Fold'; return{cards,heroPos:pos,allPos,seats,board:[],street:'Preflop', pfHist:`Folds to hero in ${pos}.`, pot:itr?`${Math.round(bb*1.5)}bb`:`$${Math.round(bb*1.5)}`,callAmt:'0', blindStr,stackStr,correct,wrong:pfWrong(correct,itr,bb),key, rangeNote:`${key} — ${inR?'✓ In RFI range for '+pos:'✗ Outside RFI range for '+pos}`, pfCtx:`Hero in ${pos} with ${key}. Folds to hero. GTO: raise or fold — no limping. Pot: ${itr?potAmt+'bb':'$'+potAmt}.`, label:'PLO Flop: facing bet with wrap draw'}; }}, {cat:'bluffing', name:'PLO river bluff or give up', build({itr,bb,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}){ const pos=randFrom(['BTN','CO']); const hand=drawPLOHand(['strong','playable']); const board=drawBoard(hand.cards,5); const potAmt=itr?bb*30:Math.round(bb*30); const correct='Give up and check (PLO river bluffs require near-nut blockers)'; return{cards:hand.cards,heroPos:pos,allPos,seats,board,street:'River', pfHist:`3-bet pot pre, c-bet flop, check turn. River: ${bStr([board[4]])}. Villain checks to hero.`, pot:itr?`${potAmt}bb`:`$${potAmt}`,callAmt:'0',blindStr,stackStr, correct,wrong:['Overbet bluff pot (polarized range)','Give up and check (PLO river bluffs require near-nut blockers)','Bet 50% pot bluff','Small block bet 33% pot'].filter(o=>o!==correct).slice(0,3), key:hand.handName, rangeNote:`${hand.handName} — PLO river bluff spot`, pfCtx:`PLO. Hero in ${pos} with ${hand.handName}. Board: ${bStr(board)}. Villain's calling range is very wide in PLO — bluffing rivers without near-nut blockers is -EV. Pot: ${itr?potAmt+'bb':'$'+potAmt}.`, label:'PLO River: bluff or give up'}; }} ]; // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // SCENARIO DISPATCHER // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ function buildScenario(cat,game,itr){ const bb=itr?100:2; const stack=itr?randFrom([20,30,40,50,60,80,100])*bb:randFrom([100,150,200,300,500]); const stackStr=itr?stack+'bb':'$'+stack; const blindStr=itr?'50/100':'1/2'; const seats=randFrom([6,6,6,8,9]); const allPos=buildPos(seats); const ctx={itr,bb,stack,stackStr,blindStr,seats,allPos}; if(game==='plo'){ const pool=cat==='preflop'?PLO_PF:[...PLO_POST.filter(t=>t.cat===cat||t.cat==='both'),...PLO_POST]; const tmpl=randFrom(pool.length?pool:PLO_POST); return{...tmpl.build(ctx),game:'PLO',variant:'PLO'}; } const pfPool=NLH_PF; const postPool=NLH_POST.filter(t=>cat==='bluffing'?t.cat==='bluffing':t.cat==='postflop'); const pool=cat==='preflop'?pfPool:(postPool.length?postPool:NLH_POST); const tmpl=randFrom(pool); return{...tmpl.build(ctx),game:'NLH',variant:"Texas Hold'em"}; } // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ // STATE & STORAGE // ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ const state={variant:'holdem',format:'cash',cat:'preflop',difficulty:'Intermediate',villain:'TAG',showPotOdds:false,sessionMode:false,sessionCount:0,sessionAnswers:[],user:null,users:[],quiz:null,selected:null,loading:false,streak:0,hintUsed:false,hint:null}; const saveUsers=u=>S.set('upc:users',u); const loadProfile=id=>S.get('upc:p:'+id); const saveProfile=(id,d)=>S.set('upc:p:'+id,d); function emptyProfile(name){return{name,sessions:0,totalQ:0,totalCorrect:0,cats:{preflop:{q:0,c:0},postflop:{q:0,c:0},bluffing:{q:0,c:0}},history:[],streakBest:0,handLog:[]};} function getKey(){return localStorage.getItem('upc_api_key')||'';} async function callClaude(sys,msg,max){ const key=getKey(); const col=isRed?'#dc2626':'#1e293b'; const sym=SYM[suit]||suit; const fs=Math.round(w*0.35); const rs=Math.round(w*0.28); const rx=Math.round(w*0.12); return ` ${rank} ${sym} ${rank}`; } function tableHTML(quiz){ const cx=300,cy=155,rx=215,ry=105; `; } async function calcEquity(){ const h1=document.getElementById('eq-h1')?.value||'',h2=document.getElementById('eq-h2')?.value||'',board=document.getElementById('eq-board')?.value||''; const res=document.getElementById('eq-result');if(!res)return; const isPLO=h1.trim().split(/\s+/).length>=4; res.innerHTML='

'; try{ const t=await callClaude(`${isPLO?'PLO':'NLH'} equity calculator. ${isPLO?'Players use exactly 2 hole cards + 3 board cards.':''} Respond ONLY valid JSON: {"hand1":{"cards":"","equity":47.3,"description":""},"hand2":{"cards":"","equity":52.7,"description":""},"ties":0.0,"analysis":"2-3 sentences."}`,`Hand 1: ${h1}\nHand 2: ${h2}\nBoard: ${board||'none'}`,600); const r=JSON.parse(t.replace(/```json|```/g,'').trim()); let html=''; [{h:r.hand1,col:'#7dd3fc'},{h:r.hand2,col:'#f9a8d4'}].forEach(item=>{html+=`
${item.h.cards}${item.h.equity}%
${item.h.description}
`;}); html+=`
${r.analysis}
`; res.innerHTML=html; }catch(e){res.innerHTML=`
Failed: ${e.message}
`;} } function renderBankroll(){ const id=state.user?.id;if(!id)return ''; const sessions=S.get('upc:br:'+id)||[]; const total=sessions.reduce((a,s)=>a+s.profit,0); const wins=sessions.filter(s=>s.profit>0).length; let html=`
`; [{l:'Profit',v:(total>=0?'+':'')+total.toFixed(2),c:total>=0?'#4ade80':'#f87171'},{l:'Sessions',v:sessions.length,c:'#1a9a9a'},{l:'Win Rate',v:sessions.length?Math.round((wins/sessions.length)*100)+'%':'—',c:'#facc15'}].forEach(s=>{html+=`
${s.l}
${s.v}
`;}); html+=`
Log Session
Date
Game

Cash-out ($)
`; [...sessions].reverse().forEach(s=>{html+=`
${s.date}${s.game?' · '+s.game+'':''}
${s.notes?`
${s.notes}
`:''}
${s.profit>=0?'+':''}${s.profit.toFixed(2)}
`;}); if(!sessions.length)html+=`
No sessions yet.
`; html+=`
`;return html; } function addSession(){ const id=state.user?.id;if(!id)return; const buyin=parseFloat(document.getElementById('br-buyin')?.value||'0'); const cashout=parseFloat(document.getElementById('br-cashout')?.value||'0'); if(!buyin||!cashout)return; const sessions=S.get('upc:br:'+id)||[]; sessions.push({id:Date.now(),date:document.getElementById('br-date')?.value||'',game:document.getElementById('br-game')?.value||'',buyin,cashout,profit:cashout-buyin,notes:document.getElementById('br-notes')?.value||''}); sessions.sort((a,b)=>new Date(a.date)-new Date(b.date)); S.set('upc:br:'+id,sessions);setTool('bankroll'); } function renderHandLog(){ const log=(state.user?.handLog||[]).slice().reverse(); let html=`
`; log.forEach(h=>{html+=`

`:''}

`;return html; } function filterHandLog(q){ q=(q||'').toLowerCase(); const log=(state.user?.handLog||[]).filter(h=>(h.question||'').toLowerCase().includes(q)).reverse(); const list=document.getElementById('hl-list');if(!list)return; let html=''; log.forEach(h=>{html+=`
